--- 帖子 #1308 ---
So here is a real time trade I am in. This is a common dilemma for everyone of us.

I am short the AUDNZD and I am in decent profit right now + 20 on the aggregate position

Now if I look at where we are on the bigger picture like 4hr and above...the answers on what to do become more clear to me and seem to fit my eye so to speak.

Even as high as the weekly just for a peek

So the decision on target is either A) take the +60 or so in front of the low @ 1.0420 OR B) Hold to see if it will break down on the bigger picture for another +350-400

-If you decide to hold, how do you trail it that makes the most sense? How much do you give back on each retracement in the belief that another lower low is coming?

- Do you just take the really easy money right now or on the next impulse down if we get one?

- There are consequences with each choice.....If you grab the easiest of money, you forego a much larger win with limited risk if any. Are you capable of sitting through a 25 -50 pip reversal against you that does nothing to change the bigger picture but you are still out those pips at least for the time being......and what if it goes another 30 after that against you.

Your ability to make these decisions with money on the table are IMHO what separates winners from losers in the long run. These are tough choices that affect your psyche. What if you exit in front of the 1.0420 number and see it fall right through and down another 150 pips in the next 2 days.....Do you beat yourself up over the what if?

Enough of this stuff for today....enjoy the ride!

--- 帖子 #1373 ---
If you are able to actively manage your trades, you will not have any need to automatically exit at a resistance level. Instead, you can watch how price reacts when it reaches that level, as it will sometimes just blow right through.

In terms of staying in a trade for the maximum amount of time, what you might find helpful is to use the Daylight Standard settings on the 5m timeframe and trade the cross of the -50 line. See chart below - you would still be in the long trade.

--- 帖子 #1385 ---
Its better you stick to at least H1 if not you will just be whipsawed out of good trades, you still need price action though is the market ranging or setting up LHs and LLs or vice-versa? Based upon your analysis you take a loss or stick with the trade.

Anything below H1 you will be taken to butchers by the Market no matter how good you are. Be patient and stick with the larger timeframes and you will get spectacular trades. Slow and steady bags you pips.

But for Indices you can still use M5.

Just in case you are still confused on the state of the market, view a higher timeframe.

--- 帖子 #1388 ---
I am not expert myself but I think your missing the whole point of divergence, divergence occurs when an indicator diverges from the market structure i.e. the market is an uptrend whilst the indicator diverges into a downtrend and vice-versa.

Attached is GBP/USD Tick1000 was making HHs then Daylight started making LHs, giving you a heads up for the massive downtrend to later come into play.

Second Chart is XAU/USD M15 with the same logic

Thats my view on Divergence Please correct me if I am wrong.

--- 帖子 #1425 ---
Nothing to be embarrassed about

In a way, yes. If I decide I'm going to trade for 4 hrs tomorrow I'll give the screen my full attention for most of that time.

I guess active trade management is just the opposite of a set and forget approach. I prefer to exit based on what's unfolding rather than using an arbitrary SL. However, I completely understand that it's not possible, or desirable, for many people.

Hello LauraT and all members.

Thank you for the great trading idea. I've seen and tested a lot of ideas. I don’t want to say they weren't good, they just didn't work well for me. But this daylight strategy is perfect for me. Just wonderful. Very easy and clear.

Attached Image (click to enlarge)
Attached Image (click to enlarge)
Attached Image (click to enlarge)

I read about the daylight scanner, but unfortunately it doesn't work. But luckily I found another scanner. That is a very big help. It gives me an acoustic signal on my mobile phone and also on my laptop. So I don't have to sit in front of the computer so long and clicking from one currency pair to the next one. This scanner is free.

Here on the chart I put 2 MAs in, just to show. (Yellow and Orange). When yellow and orange cross, comes the signal. This 2 MAs are not there when I am trading. You can play with the MAs settings and set it up according to the situation you want to be notified.

Attached Image (click to enlarge)
Attached Image (click to enlarge)

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

Care should be taken on weak market moves, often the price fails to cross the resistance and support levels. So the price goes back.
